      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kainat „ÄäHUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD„Äã" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kainat „ÄäHUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD„Äã" href="/user/show/14717996-kainat-hufflepuff-proud">Kainat „ÄäHUFFLEPUFF &amp; PROUD„Äã</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1327036383" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12365897737499957217"><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469312567ra/19804847.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Ohh, i am going to get so much hate for this! <br/>I am perfectly aware that I am in the minority here. Most of my friends adore The Wrath and the Dawn, all of my teachers (yes, I share my books with my teacher. I'm that kid) even my grandma's sister has read it AND raves about it. I honestly do not understand why, i'm afraid to ask her so i'm asking you guys. Help me please, and try not to hate me. I'm don't even know how to rate this. I don't want to give it 2 stars, because 2 stars is Queen of Sha</span>
  <span id="freeText12365897737499957217" style="display:none"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469312567ra/19804847.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ohh, i am going to get so much hate for this! <br>I am perfectly aware that I am in the minority here. Most of my friends adore The Wrath and the Dawn, all of my teachers (yes, I share my books with my teacher. I'm that kid) even my grandma's sister has read it AND raves about it. I honestly do not understand why, i'm afraid to ask her so i'm asking you guys. Help me please, and try not to hate me. I'm don't even know how to rate this. I don't want to give it 2 stars, because 2 stars is Queen of Shadow and i HATE that book! But i feel like it does not deserve 3 stars either. 2.5 it is then? Again, i don't hate this book, let's just say it's not what i expected, or wanted it to be. And if you love this then please don't let me ruin your day. I have nothing against you or your precious book, i promise. :)<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467328305ra/19580223.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I can tell most of the time if a book is for me or not, and when i saw The Wrath and the Dawn i just knew it wasn't. Especially after reading all those lovey dubby quotes made want to throw up. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467328607ra/19580245.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But my friends kept recommending this to me. I'm still not sure why. Maybe because they think i'm middle eastern (i'm Pakistani) . . . i just don't know. Finally i did some digging and came across this quote, that made me think maybe this book <i>is</i> for me and i should at least give it a try.<br><br><i>
  <b>‚ÄúI will live to see tomorrow's sunset. <br><br>Make no mistake. I swear.<br> <br>I will live to see as many sunsets as it takes.<br><br> And I will kill you. With my bare hands."</b>
</i><br><br>The thing i absolutely hated was all talk and no action. She kept repeating this again and again and again and again and again! But she never even <i>tried</i> to attack him! Mind you this is the man who has killed her best friend. And she cared for her friend enough to put her life is extreme danger and married a king who will kill her in a few hours... for what? So she can tell him some bedtime stories? And they could cuddle? Also, why exactly Khalied (did i spell his name wrong? Oh, well) likes her? When did they "fall in love"? To me it was like they absolutely loathed each other the first night, and the next thing you know, BAM! He is all over her and her love for her dead friend has flown out of the window. And i'm sitting here in utter confusion and disbelieve like, <i>
  <b>what the fuck am i reading</b>
</i>? I was actually quite disgusted with the romance. It was so wrong (not in a good way) and everything was sugar-coated and super convenient.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1467263207ra/19571150.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>
  <b>‚ÄúSo you would have me throw Shazi to the wolves?‚Äù<br>‚ÄúShazi?‚Äù Jalal‚Äôs grin widened. ‚ÄúHonestly, I pity the wolves.‚Äù</b>
</i> <br><br>Why does every single person in this book thinks so highly of our snowflake? What exactly did she do to earn this reputation? I never saw her doing anything heroic. She was arrogant, unreasonable, and foolish, sure. But I wouldn't go as far as calling her headstrong or even smart, based on what I read. I'll be honest, i knew she wasn't actually going to kill him, but i expected her to at least try! She did nothing. Literally nothing! I was so fed up with her whining and empty threats: <i>I will kill him when i'm done drooling over his hot body</i>. I couldn't care less about Khalid. I love dark characters, as long as they don't turn into love-struck puppies. *YAWN* He killed all those girls, but how can we hold that against him?! After all, he wrote letters to their families that he never even posted, so everything is fine. He has redeemed himself. Yayy! Thank god! Seriously? WTF was that?<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1469312025ra/19804812.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Every time they started talking about "love" and all that crap, i wanted to scream at the book <i> you were supposed to be trying to kill each other</i>!!! Come on, people. The other guy (forgot his name) was slightly better than these two, i guess. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/515734.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><i>(how freaking adorable is this gif?)</i><br><br>I really enjoyed Renee Ahdieh's writing style. I loved how the images she painted were so clear. I just didn't like WHAT she painted. Do i want to eat the food she painted in my head? HELL YEAH! Do i want to live in their houses? Um.. Where do i sign? I will not be continuing this series. What's the point, it's pretty obvious what's going to happen next and i am not interested. I will check out her other future books. <br>Overall thoughts:<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432572197ra/14983125.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_1136252496" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1136252496" />
    <a title="Jillian " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3101094-jillian"><img alt="Jillian " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1504472383p2/3101094.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1136252496?book_show_action=true">Dec 19, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jillian " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jillian " href="/user/show/3101094-jillian">Jillian </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1136252496" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9689002998372358716">MY FAVORITE BOOK OF THE YEAR. PERIOD. (and one of my favorite books EVER.)<br/><br/><a href='http://s102.photobucket.com/user/bookishandnerdy23/media/reviews/reviewheader_zpsyh4ab4r3.png.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432211584i/14909769._SX540_.png' alt=' photo reviewheader_zpsyh4ab4r3.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>The Wrath & The Dawn is a lush retelling of 1001 Nights. It follows Shahrzad as she seeks revenge for the murder of her best friend by The Monster King of Khorasan, Khalid.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>So I had just read ACOTAR, and I wasn't expecting another book to top for a long time this year. I was actually thinking that it would be my favorite of the year. <b>WRONG.</b> The Wrath & The Dawn hit it it out of the park for me! I was actuall</span>
  <span id="freeText9689002998372358716" style="display:none">MY FAVORITE BOOK OF THE YEAR. PERIOD. (and one of my favorite books EVER.)<br><br><a href="http://s102.photobucket.com/user/bookishandnerdy23/media/reviews/reviewheader_zpsyh4ab4r3.png.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1432211584i/14909769._SX540_.png" alt=" photo reviewheader_zpsyh4ab4r3.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>The Wrath &amp; The Dawn is a lush retelling of 1001 Nights. It follows Shahrzad as she seeks revenge for the murder of her best friend by The Monster King of Khorasan, Khalid.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>So I had just read ACOTAR, and I wasn't expecting another book to top for a long time this year. I was actually thinking that it would be my favorite of the year. <b>WRONG.</b> The Wrath &amp; The Dawn hit it it out of the park for me! I was actually really excited for this book before it came out, but I honestly wasn't expecting it to be THIS fantastic.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>Basically this is what TW&amp;TD done to me:</blockquote>
</b><br><a href="http://s102.photobucket.com/user/bookishandnerdy23/media/9577530_zps8rwnvbou.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432211584ra/14909770.gif" alt=" photo 9577530_zps8rwnvbou.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ok ok let's get to the actual review. The premise really grabbed me from the beginning, and it completely exceeded my expectations. It was perfectly paced and felt unpredictable. I was at the edge of my seat the entire time. The writing is lush and gorgeous.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"She was drowning in sandalwood and sunlight. Time ceased to more than a notion. Her lips were hers one moment. And then they were his. The taste of him on her tongue was like sun warmed honey. Like cool water sliding down her parched throat. Like the promise of all her tomorrows in one sigh."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Now if THAT doesn't make you want to read it, idk what will bruh. And yes, maybe some can say it's bit flowery and overdone, but my god how can the beautiful use of the english language this way not make you read this. Renee Ahdieh's writing is my kind of writing. Poetic, flows well, lush, and just downright lovely. It makes me want to be writer and I've never had that desire...ever until now. SO BRAVO RENEE BRAVO. <br><br>The plot is mysterious and intriguing. Yes there's this fantastic romance, but there's also this mystery as to WHY is khalid marrying a new bride every day and killing them off by dawn the next day. It hooked me from the get go as well as Shazi's plot for revenge. I also like this mysterious magic system, but I won't lie I wish I got a little more out of this aspect. I have to say the magic is till a complete mystery to me, but I hope that this will be fixed in book #2, The Rose and The Dagger.<br><br>Now let's get to the good stuff. THE ROMANCE AND THE CHARACTERS. I'm a sucker for romance. I'm gonna be straight up say I prefer all my books to have some sort of romance...even if it's subtle. This is by far one of the BEST romances I have EVER read. I ship Khalid and Shazi so hard. <br><br><a href="http://s102.photobucket.com/user/bookishandnerdy23/media/shipitlikefedex_zpsapxo7oq2.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1432211584ra/14909771.gif" alt=" photo shipitlikefedex_zpsapxo7oq2.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ahdieh's ability to captivate the readers with her words and the development of Shazi and Khalid's relationship is astounding. Did I feel conflicted over the fact that Shazi was falling for the man who killed her best friend? YES, duh. But did I believe it? ABSOLUTELY. And did Ahdieh make me root for them? WHOLEHEARTEDLY<br><br>Ok let's just talk about the characters themselves. These characters are so damn loveable. So many of these characters became some favorites of mine. Shazi is favorite MC of mine. I rolled my eyes just a tiny tiny bit at the parts where she was like I need to get revenge on this evil king, but OMG my heart is racing over him, but that's kind of the fun part of it all right? I liked that she acknowledged her conflict and struggled with it. I just love her. FAVORITE. I just wish there I got more from my side characters because I loved them. Jalal, Despina, Tariq, Rahim, Jahander, and more. I'm thinking this will be addressed more in future books because yes the romance did outweigh the development of side characters but I totally get it because this is the first book in the epic story of Khalid and Shazi. Also holla to Renee Ahdieh for putting the prologue of The Rose and The Dagger at the end. YOU DA BEST. AND I NEED THIS SEQUEL.<br><br>Overall I recommend you pick this up ASAP. Hands down, this is my favorite book of the year. Read it before it gets SUPER POPULAR. Just sayin.</span>
  <a data-text-id="9689002998372358716" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1106705454" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1106705454" />
    <a title="Andreea Pop" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4858513-andreea-pop"><img alt="Andreea Pop" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1486663526p2/4858513.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1106705454?book_show_action=true">Nov 15, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Andreea Pop" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Andreea Pop" href="/user/show/4858513-andreea-pop">Andreea Pop</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=royalty">royalty</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=funny">funny</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=i-worship-these">i-worship-these</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=high-fantasy">high-fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=read-in-2015">read-in-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=swoon-worthy-characters">swoon-worthy-characters</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=amazing-feelings">amazing-feelings</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4858513-andreea-pop?shelf=awesome-romance">awesome-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1106705454" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2206939707151129226"><i>
  <b>‚ÄúI love you, a thousand times over. And I will never apologize for it.‚Äù</b>
</i><br/><br/><i>The Wrath and the Dawn</i> is, simply put, amazing. Breathtaking. Stunning. My sappy, romantic heart was joyous with this love story, swooning and falling head over heels in love with the characters. Thrilling, seductive and incredibly enchanting, this book will have you devouring page after page filled with literary deliciousness.<br/><br/><a href='http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-wF1NEKpKPMg/VZUS7B7QJwI/AAAAAAAAPMI/bSrDF87T2DQ/s1600/843150.gif' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img height='236' src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435833281ra/15381046.gif' width='320' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> <br/><br/>One enigmatic boy-king, the caliph of Khorasan, takes a new bride every day only to have he</span>
  <span id="freeText2206939707151129226" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>‚ÄúI love you, a thousand times over. And I will never apologize for it.‚Äù</b>
</i><br><br><i>The Wrath and the Dawn</i> is, simply put, amazing. Breathtaking. Stunning. My sappy, romantic heart was joyous with this love story, swooning and falling head over heels in love with the characters. Thrilling, seductive and incredibly enchanting, this book will have you devouring page after page filled with literary deliciousness.<br><br><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-wF1NEKpKPMg/VZUS7B7QJwI/AAAAAAAAPMI/bSrDF87T2DQ/s1600/843150.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="236" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435833281ra/15381046.gif" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><br>One enigmatic boy-king, the caliph of Khorasan, takes a new bride every day only to have her killed at dawn. Madman, they call him. A ruthless, cold-blooded killer. But when Shahrzad, a sixteen-year old girl, volunteers to become his new wife, and afterwards manages the unthinkable of living the deadly dawn's arrival, things start changing pretty quickly. Especially when Shahrzad desires the caliph's head on a silver platter.<br> <br><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-yjezJHNLj8w/VZUS60kwJXI/AAAAAAAAPLw/ZF4pXRuy1dE/s1600/2357dc4635217b000050c69a1bbf8c13.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="320" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1435833281i/15381047.jpg" width="225" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Shahrzad joined my personal squad of favorite MCs. She's a feisty, fierce, silver-tongued heroine. I adored her reckless demeanor, her passionate heart and her cunning, sharp mind. And her sarcastic personality was truly a joy. Strong-willed, stubborn (but endearingly so) and clever, she was a refreshing main character. Loved her to bits. <br><br><i>
  <b>‚ÄúThis dangerous girl. This captivating beauty.<br>This destroyer of worlds and creator of wonder.‚Äù</b>
</i><br><br>Khalid, the caliph of Khorasan, the King of Kings, was swoon-worthy. You probably figured out that there's a reason he's killing his brides and the motive is absolutely soul-wrenching. But Khalid is alluring. Mercurial. Enigmatic. He's every shade of intensity known to human kind and under his cold fa√ßade, he's broken and utterly alone. His way of loving is a force to be reckoned with, one that will pretty much leave you in a pile of goo at his feet, a blubbering mess or a hyperventilating fangirl. Regardless, you will feel goosebumps and butterflies in every scene he's in, just like Shazi (a testament of the author's writing skills).<br><br><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-IycICNhjuxw/VZUS7hh5oKI/AAAAAAAAPL8/pmECUPt73U8/s1600/fa64b652254ab752ef62997cdfb1fbe5.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="320" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1435833281i/15381048.jpg" width="256" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>
  <b>‚ÄúWhat are you doing to me, you plague of a girl?‚Äù he whispered.<br>‚ÄúIf I‚Äôm a plague, then you should keep your distance, unless you plan on being destroyed.‚Äù The weapons still in her grasp, she shoved against his chest.<br>‚ÄúNo.‚Äù His hands dropped to her waist. ‚ÄúDestroy me.‚Äù</b>
</i><br><br>The actual romance was just wowza. Allow me to say it's been a while since I've read something so seductively dark in a YA book, but I'm glad this happened because <b>HOTNESS OVERLOAD</b>. These two transcended the enemies incognito phase only to reach the boundless state of mutual adoration, if you like. Because they end well past love and straight into worship land. Together, they're every bit of a royal couple, a tiger king with his queen ready to pounce on their prey. They're strong, daring and unique. Dangerous and sexy. Not to mention all-consuming. Perfect for each other and so so in love with one another that I could not suppress -- for the love of all things mighty -- a happy sigh whenever they were together. <br><br><a href="http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-zxiw89AwoWU/VZUS70IwPdI/AAAAAAAAPME/TTCHHrtj4MI/s1600/giphy.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435833281ra/15381049.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>
  <b>‚ÄúLove is‚Äîa shade of what I feel.‚Äù</b>
</i><br><br>And oh my goodness, they're sizzling, smoking hot. You'll blush, you'll drool, you'll feel your heart going bazinga at some (actually, most) of their scenes. The award for best chemistry is, hands down, theirs. <br><br>I know I basically gushed only about the romance, but there are some other elements in the story, equally enrapturing. There's a drop of magic that I really hope the author will continue to harness. Then there's the plethora of attacks at Shazi's life, just enough to put us on the edge and trigger some intriguing political repercussions. Captivating, magical and emotional, the story will pull at your heartstrings instantly and will keep you gripping the book at the same time. <br><br><a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-mst-qWhZLCk/VZUS6-ROEcI/AAAAAAAAPLs/jY4cx4givkY/s1600/d2f4f0ba9f12d1a6c7fa26176d2a2ef8.jpg" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="320" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1435833281i/15381050.jpg" width="226" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Despite the attention on their peculiar relationship, we meet other characters that have key roles in the story's development. Tariq, for instance, is such a love-sick puppy it hurt, but lovable nonetheless. Rahim and Jalal were wonderful friends and also LOL-inducing characters. And Despina was just awesome in every possible way.<br> <br><i>
  <b>‚ÄúSo you would have me throw Shazi to the wolves?‚Äù<br>‚ÄúShazi?‚Äù Jalal‚Äôs grin widened. ‚ÄúHonestly, I pity the wolves.‚Äù</b>
</i><br><br>The ending was something along the lines of OHMYGOD THIS ISN'T HAPPENING MY POOR BABY NOOO. I seriously don't know how the story will be continued -- since the series is a duology -- because all kinds of dangers are threatening Khalid, his relationship with Shazi and the kingdom he's ruling and I'm afraid they'll be too much of a burden. I can stomach all the heartbreak in the world if it means they'll get a HEA. <br><br><i>
  <b>‚ÄúMy soul sees its equal in you.‚Äù</b>
</i><br><br>Renee Ahdieh crafted this amazingly well-written debut novel in a masterful manner. She used Arabian wonders to create lush settings. She used quick and short dialogue (the type I like the most) to create realistic banter. She used different POVs to expand the story to its vast potential. And finally, she used original elements to put a glorious new spin on <i>A Thousand and One Nights</i>. Her writing-style was truly spectacular and I cannot wait to see with what she astounds us next. <br><br><i>
  <b>‚ÄúGet up, Shahrzad al-Khayzuran. You kneel before no one. Least of all me.‚Äù</b>
</i><br><br><a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-c-Z18oKdMmE/VZUS9cHSSTI/AAAAAAAAPMM/lk8OQ6YzGFw/s1600/swoon.gif" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img height="199" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1435833281ra/15381051.gif" width="320" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I beg you to abandon your endless TBR and pick up <i>The Wrath and the Dawn</i>. Lose yourself in its mesmerizing tale, have your heart crushed in between its pages and witness Shazi and Khalid become the epitome of romance. I promise this exquisite and soul-wrenching story will be among your new favorites. Just don't kill me for waiting a year for the sequel -- I am agonizing by myself quite alright. <br><br><b>ENJOY! &lt;3</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="2206939707151129226" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<tr class="no_border feedFooterReview" id="update_comment_stuff_Review1377666240">

  <span id="freeText14199586721056723774" style="display:none">‚ù• ùüú.ùüù/‚òÖ‚òÖ‚òÖ‚òÖ‚òÖ <br /><br />‚Äúùó°ùóº. ùó¨ùóºùòÇ ùòÄùó≤ùó≤ ùòÅùóµùó∂ùóªùó¥ùòÄ ùòÅùóµùó≤ ùòÑùóÆùòÜ ùòÜùóºùòÇ ùóπùó∂ùòÉùó≤ ùòÜùóºùòÇùóø ùóπùó∂ùó≥ùó≤. ùó™ùó∂ùòÅùóµùóºùòÇùòÅ ùó≥ùó≤ùóÆùóø."<br /><br />ùó™ùóºùóøùóπùó± ùóØùòÇùó∂ùóπùó±ùó∂ùóªùó¥<br />You travel through so many stories in this book. The stories range from wrath to revenge and dawn to love. I liked how the fairytales mixed with this book, it reminded me of aladdin and the magic lamp. I know they are different but the settings were similar and I loved it.<br /><br />‚ÄúùôÑùô£ ùô¢ùôÆ ùô°ùôûùôõùôö, ùô©ùôùùôö ùô§ùô£ùôö ùô©ùôùùôûùô£ùôú ùôÑ ùôùùôñùô´ùôö ùô°ùôöùôñùôßùô£ùôöùôô ùôñùôóùô§ùô´ùôö ùôñùô°ùô° ùôûùô® ùô©ùôùùôñùô© ùô£ùô§ ùôûùô£ùôôùôûùô´ùôûùôôùô™ùôñùô° ùôòùôñùô£ ùôßùôöùôñùôòùôù ùô©ùôùùôö ùôùùôöùôûùôúùôùùô© ùô§ùôõ ùô©ùôùùôöùôûùôß ùô•ùô§ùô©ùôöùô£ùô©ùôûùôñùô° ùô¨ùôûùô©ùôùùô§ùô™ùô© ùô©ùôùùôö ùô°ùô§ùô´ùôö ùô§ùôõ ùô§ùô©ùôùùôöùôßùô®."<br /><br />ùêëùê®ùê¶ùêöùêßùêúùêû<br />Do you want to read a enemies to lovers romance book mixed with retellings that melt and break your heart at the same time? If so I'm going to recommend this book to you. From enemies to lovers, we read about a man with a lost soul and a woman with a heart as bright as the sun and they both desire, one for revenge and one for death. But every dawn these desires lead them to each other in different ways, from moonlight til dawn they find the meaning of true love through the stories. With each dawn, they fall more in love and understand each other better and they write their own love story, the story of pain and love. <br /><br />‚ÄúùôÑùôõ ùôÆùô§ùô™ ùô¨ùô§ùô™ùô°ùôô, ùôúùôûùô´ùôö ùôùùôûùô¢ ùô©ùôùùôö ùô°ùô§ùô´ùôö ùô©ùôùùôñùô© ùô¨ùôûùô°ùô° ùôöùô£ùôñùôóùô°ùôö ùôùùôûùô¢ ùô©ùô§ ùô®ùôöùôö ùôûùô© ùôõùô§ùôß ùôùùôûùô¢ùô®ùôöùô°ùôõ. ùôèùô§ ùôñ ùô°ùô§ùô®ùô© ùô®ùô§ùô™ùô°, ùô®ùô™ùôòùôù ùôñ ùô©ùôßùôöùôñùô®ùô™ùôßùôö ùôûùô® ùô¨ùô§ùôßùô©ùôù ùôûùô©ùô® ùô¨ùôöùôûùôúùôùùô© ùôûùô£ ùôúùô§ùô°ùôô. ùôíùô§ùôßùô©ùôù ùôûùô©ùô® ùô¨ùôöùôûùôúùôùùô© ùôûùô£ ùôôùôßùôöùôñùô¢ùô®.‚Äù<br /><br />ùó¶ùòÅùóºùóøùòÜùóπùó∂ùóªùó≤/ ùó∂ùó±ùó≤ùóÆ / ùòÑùóøùó∂ùòÅùó∂ùóªùó¥ ùòÄùòÅùòÜùóπùó≤<br />The storyline teaches you to know how your actions can affect the live of others. And you must think before you act and decide wisely so that it doesn't cost you anything.<br />The story idea and the plot was new and beautiful for me and I loved every fairytale that was used in this book. But I wish I could see more magic in it. The descriptions were so beautiful and I was drowned in the beauty of her writing.<br /> <br />‚Äúùôéùô§ùô¢ùôö ùô©ùôùùôûùô£ùôúùô® ùôöùô≠ùôûùô®ùô© ùôûùô£ ùô§ùô™ùôß ùô°ùôûùô´ùôöùô® ùôõùô§ùôß ùôóùô™ùô© ùôñ ùôóùôßùôûùôöùôõ ùô¢ùô§ùô¢ùôöùô£ùô©. ùòºùô£ùôô ùô¨ùôö ùô¢ùô™ùô®ùô© ùô°ùôöùô© ùô©ùôùùôöùô¢ ùôúùô§ ùô§ùô£ ùô©ùô§ ùô°ùôûùôúùôùùô© ùôñùô£ùô§ùô©ùôùùôöùôß ùô®ùô†ùôÆ."<br /><br />ùóñùóµùóÆùóøùóÆùó∞ùòÅùó≤ùóøùòÄ<br /><br />ùë∫ùíâùíÇùíâùíìùíõùíÇùíÖ<br />I like girls with rude, stubborn and arrogant personalities, including Shahrzad. I loved her stories and the way she did whatever she wanted. And although she knew she might die, she wasn't afraid. At first, sometimes she was a bit annoying because she judged Khalid without knowing him and I didn't like what she called him. But when she tried to understand and know him, everything went very well. I liked the way she loved Khalid and how her love was beyond words, like he was the reason she was breathing. <br /><br />ùë≤ùíâùíÇùíçùíäùíÖ<br />We see a man with a broken heart and a ruined soul. A man with so much weight on his shoulders that takes his breath and kills him every day. A dead person with no hope for future and happiness that looking for love. I loved how Ren√©e Ahdieh gave Khalid a reason to breath, live and exist and lets him find his soul and the light of his life with Shahrzad. Shahrzad shows him that only he can choose who he wants to be. It was like "Give me your light, something more than love and I give you my all. Because Love is a miracle that can break any curse." I admire Khalid's love and his caring. the way he valued and protected her from everything, it was so beautiful, it was like nothing more valuable than Shahrzad existed in the world, like his love for her was ‚Äåall he wanted in life and Shahrzad was his everything. <br /><br />ùë±ùíÇùíçùíÇùíç<br />I loved his personality, the kindness, warmth and his protective attitude towards his family was everything.<br /><br />ùëªùíÇùíìùíäùíí<br />I didn‚Äôt like him but I hope I know him better in the next book.<br /><br />ùó†ùòÜ ùó≥ùó≤ùó≤ùóπùó∂ùóªùó¥ùòÄ:<br />I liked this book, its characters, the world building, the idea and everything about it. Especially the writing style, it was amazing and I enjoyed it so much. <br /><br />(***Sorry if my review wasn‚Äôt good, This is the first time I have written such a complete review.)<br /><br />ùòòùò∂ùò∞ùòµùò¶ùò¥: <br />‚Äúùôãùôöùô§ùô•ùô°ùôö ùôõùôñùô°ùô° ùôûùô£ ùôñùô£ùôô ùô§ùô™ùô© ùô§ùôõ ùô°ùô§ùô´ùôö ùô¨ùôûùô©ùôù ùô©ùôùùôö ùôßùôûùô®ùôûùô£ùôú ùôñùô£ùôô ùô®ùôöùô©ùô©ùôûùô£ùôú ùô§ùôõ ùô©ùôùùôö ùô®ùô™ùô£.‚Äù<br /><br />‚Äúùó™ùóµùó≤ùóª ùóú ùòÑùóÆùòÄ ùóÆ ùóπùó∂ùòÅùòÅùóπùó≤ ùó¥ùó∂ùóøùóπ ùó∂ùóª ùóßùóµùó≤ùóØùó≤ùòÄ, ùóú ùóøùó≤ùó∫ùó≤ùó∫ùóØùó≤ùóø ùóÆùòÄùó∏ùó∂ùóªùó¥ ùó∫ùòÜ ùó∫ùóºùòÅùóµùó≤ùóø ùòÑùóµùóÆùòÅ ùóµùó≤ùóÆùòÉùó≤ùóª ùòÑùóÆùòÄ. ùó¶ùóµùó≤ ùóøùó≤ùóΩùóπùó∂ùó≤ùó±, ‚Äòùóî ùóµùó≤ùóÆùóøùòÅ ùòÑùóµùó≤ùóøùó≤ ùóπùóºùòÉùó≤ ùó±ùòÑùó≤ùóπùóπùòÄ." <br />‚Äúùóú ùòÅùóµùó≤ùóª ùó±ùó≤ùó∫ùóÆùóªùó±ùó≤ùó± ùòÅùóº ùó∏ùóªùóºùòÑ ùòÑùóµùóÆùòÅ ùó∞ùóºùóªùòÄùòÅùó∂ùòÅùòÇùòÅùó≤ùó± ùóµùó≤ùóπùóπ. ùó¶ùóµùó≤ ùóπùóºùóºùó∏ùó≤ùó± ùó∫ùó≤ ùòÄùòÅùóøùóÆùó∂ùó¥ùóµùòÅ ùó∂ùóª ùòÅùóµùó≤ ùó≤ùòÜùó≤ ùóÆùóªùó± ùòÄùóÆùó∂ùó±, ‚Äòùóî ùóµùó≤ùóÆùóøùòÅ ùóÆùóØùòÄùó≤ùóªùòÅ ùóπùóºùòÉùó≤.‚Äù</span>

<div id="review_1417669377" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1417669377" />
    <a title="Dorreh" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/22599584-dorreh"><img alt="Dorreh" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1565727363p2/22599584.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1417669377?book_show_action=true">Oct 15, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dorreh" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dorreh" href="/user/show/22599584-dorreh">Dorreh</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1417669377" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16976539901152356696">Okay to begin by saying this book was glorious is pure injustice. But I will say that this story was a waft of fresh air in the young adult trivia. The story takes place in the ancient city of khorasan, in a time of magic and mystical existence. Maybe one of the main reasons I loved this book so much was the use of Persian origin words. My mother tongue being Farsi, this book felt like home. Like I was reading a story about my people and my history, even though it leaned more towards the influen</span>
  <span id="freeText16976539901152356696" style="display:none">Okay to begin by saying this book was glorious is pure injustice. But I will say that this story was a waft of fresh air in the young adult trivia. The story takes place in the ancient city of khorasan, in a time of magic and mystical existence. Maybe one of the main reasons I loved this book so much was the use of Persian origin words. My mother tongue being Farsi, this book felt like home. Like I was reading a story about my people and my history, even though it leaned more towards the influences of Pakistani culture. The scenes, the food, especially the LAVASH bread, the use of words like "Joonam" and "delam" made me even more connected to the characters and everything in the book itself.<br /><br />Renee ahdieh is a magnificent storyteller, she used the idea of a classical Arabian tale and transformed it into a story of love and betrayal. Her main character shahrzad(also a common Persian name) is everything I look for in a strong willed and blazing female character, and as for Khalid......well.....who doesn't love a tragically broken boy with the weight of the world on his shoulders? *mentally screeches over the love scenes*. The story not only presents characters and their internal and external struggles, but I personally feel that all the side characters of this story had a constructive role to maintain. <br /><br />One of my absolute favorites is jalal and despina. For every single time jalal did something to support the forsaken love between the monster and the silver tongue, I had a small melt down (the good kind). <br />I think on the list of things that I loved in this story, and that is a very long list indeed, the topper would be the element of physical strength that came alongside the strength of will. When shahrzad picked up the bow and arrow and just flew through 500 stages of awesome, I was fully entrapped in my growing love for her character. This love flourished when she picked up a sword she has never wielded, to get the answers she wanted. I just likem bold as they come.<br />I flew through the pages of this book, I honestly was reeking of curiosity to simply know what happens next. Many authors are gifted enough to create a story that you want to finish because you just need to know what happens next, but not all of them can so intricately create a world that absorbs you and absolves you so delicately. <br />I might just not make it in this unfathomable need to read the sequel, I highly recommend this book to anyone who simply can read............</span>
  <a data-text-id="16976539901152356696" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_929112493" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/929112493" />
    <a title="Steph Sinclair" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4642710-steph-sinclair"><img alt="Steph Sinclair" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1457555690p2/4642710.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/929112493?book_show_action=true">May 05, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Steph Sinclair" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Steph Sinclair" href="/user/show/4642710-steph-sinclair">Steph Sinclair</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=young-adult">young-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=print-arc">print-arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=marginalized-stories">marginalized-stories</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=penguin">penguin</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=fantasy">fantasy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=strong-heroine">strong-heroine</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=may">may</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=alternating-povs">alternating-povs</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=beautiful-prose">beautiful-prose</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4642710-steph-sinclair?shelf=cool-author">cool-author</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer929112493" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12518559994445205980"><b>Actual rating is somewhere around 3.5 stars.</b><br/><br/><em>The Wrath and the Dawn</em> has all the elements of an amazing story. It has a strong heroine, intriguing plot, moral ambiguity, a complex cast of characters that inspire all sorts of internal emotional turmoil. Basically, set phasers to LET ME LOVE YOU. Even for those like me who haven't read <em>A Thousand and One Nights</em>, can appreciate the rich setting and visually stunning descriptions. And I can't tell you how happy I am to say that I really enjoyed <em>The Wr</em></span>
  <span id="freeText12518559994445205980" style="display:none"><b>Actual rating is somewhere around 3.5 stars.</b><br /><br /><em>The Wrath and the Dawn</em> has all the elements of an amazing story. It has a strong heroine, intriguing plot, moral ambiguity, a complex cast of characters that inspire all sorts of internal emotional turmoil. Basically, set phasers to LET ME LOVE YOU. Even for those like me who haven't read <em>A Thousand and One Nights</em>, can appreciate the rich setting and visually stunning descriptions. And I can't tell you how happy I am to say that I really enjoyed <em>The Wrath and the Dawn</em> and I'm hoping many of my friends will give it a chance.<br /><br />Sharhrzad (Shazi), desperate to¬†avenge her best friend's murder, decides to volunteer as tribute to be the next wife of the¬†Caliph of Khorasan,¬†Khalid. He's known as a ruthless ruler, who kills all his wives at dawn the day after he weds. Why is a mystery to everyone including Shazi, who really doesn't care either way, and I don't blame her. Of course, as the reader can surmise from the synopsis, there's something more going on than meets the eye. As Shazi gets to know Khalid, she learns he's not what she thought he'd be and is conflicted that she finds it increasingly difficult to hate him, and more importantly, to kill him. And while that is all going on, we have Tariq, who, for all intents and purposes, was Shazi's boyfriend/betrothed before she took on the suicidal task of killing the Caliph. He struggles with his own feelings of Shazi's impending death (really, no one expected her to live to see the day after her wedding night) and is determined to rescue her at all costs. Little does he know, Shazi falls in love with Khalid and things get a little... messy.<br /><br />Told in a 3rd person point-of-view, <em>The Wrath and the Dawn</em> seeks to cover a lot of story, which it both succeeds and fails at. I'm not usually a fan of 3rd person because it makes me feel detached from the characters and their feelings, but in this case, it worked out well for me. The reader is able to get a good feel on all the characters' intentions and struggles, and that's a feat consider how many characters are introduced over the course of this novel.<br /><br />The downside to this is that I wasn't able to fully connect with any characters on an emotional level, let alone the romance, because it simply didn't get much page time. For that reason, I would have preferred for this book to have been longer OR less page time for the supporting cast for at least the first half so that I could see Shazi and Khalid's interactions more. I didn't have enough build up to have the emotional response lines like these should have set off:<br /><blockquote>‚ÄúMy soul sees its equal in you.‚Äù</blockquote><br />And...<br /><blockquote>‚ÄúLove is‚Äîa shade of what I feel.‚Äù</blockquote><br />Believe me when I say these were beautiful scenes, but I didn't swoon, and that makes me rather sad.¬†Currently, the romance is getting huge praise¬†from other reviewers, so your milage may vary, but, I felt it lacked a certain spark.<br /><br />The writing itself is very lovely and flows in a magical fashion befitting the setting of the novel. Ahdieh's set the perfect tone with her descriptions and the dialogue was both thought provoking and witty a good portion of the time. Some of my favorite lines came from Despina, Shazi's handmaiden:<br /><blockquote>‚ÄúWe women are a sad lot, aren't we?"<br />"What do you mean?"<br />"Strong enough to take on the world with our bare hands, yet we permit ridiculous boys to make fools of us."<br />"I am not a fool."<br />"No, you're not. Not yet.‚Äù</blockquote><br />This is probably why 3rd person worked so well in <em>The Wrath and the Dawn.</em>¬†The characters and their interactions always felt genuine and personable and not flat like cardboard. They weren't always likable, especially Khalid with his tug-a-war like personality, but he was consistently complex. I would guess that my feelings toward him mirrored Shazi's frustration at his lack of trust. He spends much of his time trying to atone for what he's done, but can't bring himself to fully trust her with his secret and the reason behind the deaths of his previous wives.<br /><br />Yet, while beautiful and lush in its own right, <em>The Wrath and the Dawn</em> is not without its faults. You do have your obligatory mentions of the love interest's eyes and how the female main character seems to be the only one to ever truly bring the love interest out of his broken shell. The former is what bothered me the most throughout the novel simply because I couldn't really see what it was about Shazi that he was drawn to. Was it her snarky bluntness? Her beauty? The fact that he didn't understand why she volunteered to be his wife, knowing what her fate would be? I have no idea. I was also a bit surprised (and disappointed?) that Shazi's only plan to survive the dawn was to tell the Caliph a story and deliberately end it on a cliffhanger as the sun rose to generate anticipation from Khalid. Well, okay. It certainly gives new meaning to stories having power, that's for sure. [Again, I haven't read <i>A Thousand and One Nights</i>]<br /><br />Then there¬†were times when Shazi felt deliberately obtuse when it came to Khalid and his secrets. When there were multiple attempts on her life and Khalid himself jumps to save her and reprimand those who tried to do her bodily harm, she still continues to blame him for the attempts. That seemed odd and out of character for Shazi since she is written as very observant and sharp. To her credit, she does start to question happenings¬†shortly after, but this misstep felt too contrived and forced.<br /><br />The final 30% is where this novel truly shined for me since all chips are laid out on the table and characters' true intentions are revealed. I admit to being pleasantly surprised and saddened by one in particular. The stakes will definitely be higher in the sequel, <em>
  <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/23308084-the-rose-and-the-dagger" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">The Rose and the Dagger</a>
</em>¬†and I look forward to seeing things get complicated. Also, I'm really hoping for a magic carpet ride.<br /><br />All in all, <em>The Wrath and the Dawn</em> is a strong start to a promising new series. The pros in the novel far outweigh the small cons, which could admittedly be attributed to my cynical mind and lack of a functioning heart. Don't let that stop you from picking this up.<br /><br /><i>ARC was received from the author in exchange for review.</i><br /><br />More reviews and other fantastical things at <a href="http://cuddlebuggery.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Cuddlebuggery</a>.</span>
  <a data-text-id="12518559994445205980" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2071505820" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5369107921086082582">There's webcomic adaptation of this book (under the same name) out on Webtoons now! The art made by Silvester Vitale. I've alread read through the episodes that are up and it's amazng! Be sure to check it out too. <3<br/><br/><br/>**************************************<br/><br/>*4.5/5 stars*<br/><br/><i>
  <b>‚ÄúA true plague of a girl. And yet a queen in every sense of the word.‚Äù</b>
</i><br/><br/>Such a beautifully written fairy tale. I loved the story, the romance and how the world was depicted. I had some problems here and there, but it was just such </span>
  <span id="freeText5369107921086082582" style="display:none">There's webcomic adaptation of this book (under the same name) out on Webtoons now! The art made by Silvester Vitale. I've alread read through the episodes that are up and it's amazng! Be sure to check it out too. &lt;3<br /><br /><br />**************************************<br /><br />*4.5/5 stars*<br /><br /><i>
  <b>‚ÄúA true plague of a girl. And yet a queen in every sense of the word.‚Äù</b>
</i><br /><br />Such a beautifully written fairy tale. I loved the story, the romance and how the world was depicted. I had some problems here and there, but it was just such an enticing quiet tale. <br />Exquisite writing style. Compelling change of POVs. Delicious food. Descriptions of clothes and culture. A few moments which tug at some heartstrings. Great female friendship (loved Despina) and addictive romance. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>‚ÄúShe was a dangerous, dangerous girl. A plague. A Mountain of Adamant who tore the iron from ships, sinking them to their watery graves without a second thought. With a mere smile and a wrinkle of her nose.‚Äù</b>
</i><br /><br />I had some problems with the pace, it was mostly slower read until the last part of the book, which I couldn't stop reading. I loved the flowery writing style and think it really fits the story, but I know that it's not for everyone. It took me some time to warm to Khalid's character, but when I did I fell in love with him and Shahrzad. <br /><br /><i>
  <b>‚ÄúIt‚Äôs a fitting punishment for a monster. to want something so much‚Äîto hold it in your arms ‚Äî and know beyond a doubt you will never deserve it.‚Äù</b>
</i><br /><br />Shahrzad is a great heroine. Sometimes her behavior was a bit spoiled, though not enough for me to dislike her. I kept hearing in reviews how intelligent and cunning Shazi is and while I do think she is clever, I expect more from her in the sequel. <br />Despina and Jalal were a great duo. I wasn't the biggest fan of Tariq and the promise of a love triangle. I have my ship and don't want anyone to to get in the way of it.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>‚ÄúMy soul sees its equal in you.‚Äù</b>
</i><br /><br />All in all, a beautiful story with rich descriptions of food, clothing and culture, obviously very much romance centered, with mostly slow pace and intrigue. Hopefully, I will enjoy the sequel just as much.<br /><br /><i>
  <b>‚ÄúWe women are a sad lot, aren't we?"<br />"What do you mean?"<br />"Strong enough to take on the world with our bare hands, yet we permit ridiculous boys to make fools of us."<br />"I am not a fool."<br />"No, you're not. Not yet.‚Äù</b>
</i><br /><br /><br /><i>
  <b>‚ÄúSo you would have me throw Shazi to the wolves?‚Äù<br />‚ÄúShazi?‚Äù Jalal‚Äôs grin widened. ‚ÄúHonestly, I pity the wolves.‚Äù</b>
</i><br /><br /><br />************************************<br /><br />I'm very excited for this one! Hopefully the inside of this book will be just as stunning as the outside is! ‚ô•<br /><br />My first <i>A Thousand and One Nights</i> retelling, here we go!<br /><br />Buddy read with the lovely <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/19846410-ivusha" rel="nofollow noopener">Ivusha</a>.</span>
  <a data-text-id="5369107921086082582" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1411608395" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7478082186048011171"><b>2 stars? 3.5 stars? 5 STARS?!?!</b><br/><br/>Fucked if I know. I'm...torn. So I guess I'll leave this at three stars for now. <br/><br/>This book made me feel a lot of feels. But they were conflicting feels. On the one hand, this is a beautifully written, atmospheric 1001 Nights retelling rich with imagery. On the other hand, a lot of that gorgeous prose is dedicated to showing the reader, over and over again, how indecisive the female lead is. <br/><br/>You see, she's chosen to marry the king out of vengeance. He married and ki</span>
  <span id="freeText7478082186048011171" style="display:none"><b>2 stars? 3.5 stars? 5 STARS?!?!</b><br /><br />Fucked if I know. I'm...torn. So I guess I'll leave this at three stars for now. <br /><br />This book made me feel a lot of feels. But they were conflicting feels. On the one hand, this is a beautifully written, atmospheric 1001 Nights retelling rich with imagery. On the other hand, a lot of that gorgeous prose is dedicated to showing the reader, over and over again, how indecisive the female lead is. <br /><br />You see, she's chosen to marry the king out of vengeance. He married and killed her best friend, along with countless other young women, and she's bent on putting an end to his bloody reign by sticking a knife in his chest. Or a sword in his gullet. Or by bludgeoning him over the head with a mace. Or by slipping a bit of poison into his...well, you get the picture. <br /><br />That's all well and good, if you actually CARRY OUT THE DEED. But our female lead doesn't do that. Instead, she spends the first half of this book being a whiny, wishy-washy pain in the ass, failing to kill him even though she's provided with multiple opportunities to do so. <br /><br />All because he's pretteh. <br /><br />-_____-<br /><br />So was Stalin. It doesn't make him any less of a murderous bastard. <br /><br />I would have enjoyed her character so much more had she remained stalwart. Had she remained loyal to all those dead women and simply tried and failed to kill him. Repeatedly. Until she was forced to look past that pretty face and that cold facade to the troubled soul beneath. Because only in the latter half of this book do you begin to understand Shahrzad's unfortunate attraction to him. Only then do you begin to wonder why he's done the things that he has, and want, no, <i>need</i> to know the truth behind his actions. <br /><br />Still...I'll be reading the next one. The writing alone makes it worth it. Even if I spend the entirety of the second installment trapped in the same frustrated emotional state that I was forced to endure throughout this one. <br /><br />And that should tell you something. <br /><br /><b><a href="http://www.thealliterates.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">Blog</a> | <a href="https://www.facebook.com/thealliterates/" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a> | <a href="https://twitter.com/thealliterates" rel="nofollow noopener">Twitter</a> | <a href="https://www.instagram.com/the_alliterates/" rel="nofollow noopener">Instagram</a> | <a href="https://www.pinterest.com/thealliterates/" rel="nofollow noopener">Pinterest</a></b></span>
  <a data-text-id="7478082186048011171" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2340090306?book_show_action=true">May 04, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Reynita Maharani ‚òÖ The Night Reader ‚òÖ" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Reynita Maharani ‚òÖ The Night Reader ‚òÖ" href="/user/show/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader">Reynita Maharani ‚òÖ The Night Reader ‚òÖ</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Paperback " href="/book/show/32370233-the-wrath-the-dawn">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=breath-in-breath-out">breath-in-breath-out</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=i-love-the-cover">i-love-the-cover</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=heroines-i-can-relate-to">heroines-i-can-relate-to</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/43850323-reynita-maharani-the-night-reader?shelf=i-even-thought-to-not-finish-it">i-even-thought-to-not-finish-it</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2340090306" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7939867504781198893"><b>3.8 STARS</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><br/>"Don't sneer at me. I may be small, but, when pushed, I can <br/>strike out with a surprising amount of force."<br/></i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><br/>Before I begin reviewing the book, I want to say a massive thank you to <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/5743835' rel='nofollow noopener'>My friend Brittany</a> for telling me about the romance in this book because if you didn't tell me, then I wouldn't buy this book in the first place and also thank you for listening to my thoughts about this book through messages! <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1526203665ra/25531314.gif' width='350' height='160' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <u>My Opinion Time!</u>
</b><br/><br/>The reasons that I read this because Brittany told me </span>
  <span id="freeText7939867504781198893" style="display:none"><b>3.8 STARS</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><br>"Don't sneer at me. I may be small, but, when pushed, I can <br>strike out with a surprising amount of force."<br></i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br>Before I begin reviewing the book, I want to say a massive thank you to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/5743835" rel="nofollow noopener">My friend Brittany</a> for telling me about the romance in this book because if you didn't tell me, then I wouldn't buy this book in the first place and also thank you for listening to my thoughts about this book through messages! <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1526203665ra/25531314.gif" width="350" height="160" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>My Opinion Time!</u>
</b><br><br>The reasons that I read this because Brittany told me about the romance and I also felt the need to read all of Ahdieh's books or at least try reading them and it's all because of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1952315775?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Flame in the Mist</a>, I loved that book so much! So, This book is a retelling of <i>One Thousand and One Nights</i> and to be honest, I haven't read <i>One Thousand and One Nights.</i><br><br>When I decided to read this book, I had these high expectations about the book and <b>HOW COULD I NOT?</b> when I loved the other book of the author so much but then surprisingly, I didn't enjoy reading it at first because I expected a lot of actions and there was too much talking and I <b>ACTUALLY</b> thought to dnf the book because <b>AT FIRST</b> I couldn't relate to Shahrzad and then Khalid was cold, too distant, bland and boring but then it all changed. It all changed when I was on page 103. My interest in reading it more began from this page and I had never been bored anymore since page 103. So it took me a quite long time to connect myself to the story of the book and relate to Shahrzad and the romance. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1526213026ra/25532633.gif" width="270" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Another thing that fascinated me about Ahdieh's books is that I constantly need a dictionary with me while reading her books because every time I read her books, I often open a dictionary to know the meaning of some words and it happens so constantly to the point that I always put my phone beside me while reading her books and I'm actually happy because this way I can improve my english vocabulary. ( English is not my first language but I have been very interested to learn it and actively studying it since I was 8 years old ). <br><br>AND I HAVE NO IDEA HOW MANY TIMES I CRIED WHILE READING THIS BOOK. OH MY GOD. It's not only the plot that made me cry but it's also because of the writing style. I don't like flowery writing style or a very beautiful writing style and don't ask me why because I don't even know. lol. But I totally love Ahdieh's writing style because her writing style is beautiful but not overly for me and so many lines written by her make feel as if those lines stab me in the heart and make my eyes teary and cry. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i><br>"When I was a little girl in Thebes, I <br>remember asking my mother what heaven was. She replied,'A<br>heart where love dwells.' Of course, I then demanded to know <br>what constituted hell. She looked me straight in the eye and said, <br>'A heart absent love.'"<br>(page 209)<br></i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b><br>"Some things exist in our lives for but a brief moment. And <br>we must let them go on to light another sky."<br>(page 296)<br></b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>There are many more lines in the book that make me cry and please read the book yourself, you won't regret it or maybe even though you don't end up liking it in the end, at least you have tried reading it. I don't know how but Ahdieh's writing style always makes my eyes teary and makes me clutch my chest on one hand and stifle tears. This is why I love her writing style. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1476354909ra/20830692.gif" width="220" height="160" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <u>The Romance and The Characters</u>
</b><br><br>Actually, I wanted to read this book years ago but then I knew there was a love triangle in this book and that prevented me from reading it because <b>I LOATH A LOVE TRIANGLE SO MUCH.</b>But then Brittany told me and explained me about the romance and I was convinced to read it and after I read it, I can say that the love triangle in this book is the kind of love triangle that I can tolerate. I won't go into full detail about it but I'm just gonna explain it briefly. So the MC has a first love but we don't see many scenes between them and the MC barely thinks about him and the MC is not the kind of character that I absolutely hate in a love triangle situation. The kind of character that is torn between two people ( God. That is why I hate a love triangle. It's so annoying. ugh ) because in my opinion, this doesn't happen in the book. The MC even rarely think about her first love and then she falls for another man. So, if you are like me, you hate a love triangle, then don't worry. The love triangle in this book is not bad. For me, it's tolerable. <br><br>AND OH MY GOD. THE ROMANCE IN THIS BOOK. It's enemy to lover. MY FAVORITE TROPE. *squeals in delight* It's so good! and It literally made me sobbing and I don't sob often while reading books these days but THIS BOOK managed to make me sobbing. Oh my God. Every time I read this certain scene, I always find myself swiping my wet cheeks due to the tears. I could feel the romance and the spark of romance between them. I often found myself smiling because it's so sweet and romantic and there was no single scene that I found cheesy. Every romance scenes between the MC and her love interest were all hot, romantic and sweet. It's really good!<br><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1526218132ra/25532946.gif" width="270" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>There is only one person that I <s>hated</s> hate so much. It's <i>the other guy</i> like wtf, just stay away and I hate this person so much and every time he spoke ill or even thought badly about MC's love interest, I felt as if there was a fire inside me and my blood was boiling and I wanted to punched this guy so badly. THE MC'S LOVE INTEREST IS BETTER THAN HIM. HE IS NOTHING COMPARED TO HIM AND I HATE HIM SO MUCH. Every time I read his POV, I rolled my eyes and then I also counted how many pages left I had to suffer by reading his POV. Yes, my friends, I hate him <i>that</i> much. I FUCKING hate him so much Oh and If I only I got the chance to speak to this guy, I would totally say this : <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1458505896ra/18496136.gif" width="290" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and the secondary characters in this book were all amazing! My favorites are Jalal and Despina. They made me laugh and smirk and giggle so many times. Just read the book and you'll know what I'm talking about. I love them! <br><br>Thank you so much for reading and liking this review! I appreciate it so much, guys. I hope you all have an amazing day! &lt;3 <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1472831616ra/20315973.gif" width="270" height="170" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢<br><br><b>REVIEW TO COME.</b> <br><br>‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢‚Ä¢<br><b>I'm reading this book because : <br><br>1. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/5743835" rel="nofollow noopener">My friend Brittany</a> told me about the romance of the book and I feel intrigued to know more. <br>2. I loved Flame in the Mist so much. <br>3. I need to read all Ahdieh's books or at least try reading them. <br><br>Have you guys read this book? And what do you think of it? ( no spoiler, please! ) </b></span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('jIdfZfLUnLMQ5frjJcOhCOcgRkvhQFwWUW4EHzZccA8+xH+716AEZel/UEazQijgSmYC5jSKe3tfL+MCmKYatQ==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('7/h4ypB3cc/rEDs/NpnOi/NFrkz6Y2rGnBZ2fCcDqlddu1gUtQPpGRKKkZqgGEdjXgPq4S+pTauSV5FhifnA7Q==')})
  }
//]]>
